# For Apache 2.2 Use
<IfModule !mod_authz_core.c>
	<IfModule mod_authz_host.c>
		Order allow,deny
		Allow from all
		Deny from env=spambot
	</IfModule>
</IfModule>


# For Apache 2.4 Use
<IfModule mod_authz_core.c>
	<RequireAll>
		Require all granted
		Require not env spambot
	</RequireAll>
</IfModule>
